instruction is not counted.

## Optimization (Tier 2) stats

<details>
<summary> statistics about the Tier 2 optimizer </summary>

<table>
<thead>
<tr>
<th align="left"></th>
<th align="right">Count</th>
<th align="right">Ratio</th>
</tr>
</thead>
<tbody>
<tr>
<td align="left">
Optimization attempts
